NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

No. 2130/108/109, Tamil Nadu Housing Board, Ayyapakkam, Chennai-600 077,  has been living as Male. I have been granted 
Third gender Identity Card No. 044/21. Issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department.
By this, I may treated as Male and shall henceforth be known as J. JOSHUA JAYDEN.
Chennai,
